297a6(1): mi shes pa mthong bar gyur pa ni/ byang chub kyi phyogs rnams kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun pa rnams kyis brgyan pa'i sku gser gyi phung por
297b1(1): mngag 'dra bar nga 'bar bar gyur pas/ 'dag rten gyi khams rnams cad du na pa ma da pal ba tuzhugs pa'i 'dzi rten pa rnams kyi mig tu gyu bas/ 'khar ba khrag du ma rnams
297b2(1): la 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi'i gtam dang yang dag par ldan pa ston par mdzad do// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa'i mdo rdzogs s+ho// 
297b3(1): / rgya gar skad du/ rang thal/ swastaM gathA/ bod skad du/ dkon mchog gsum gyi bde legs tshigs su bcad pa// dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// 
297b4(1): sangs rgyas gcol yon tan mchog mnga' ba// che dgus mchod cing smon lam sprin tshogs 'dus// go phang mchog rnyed bstong pa'i char 'bebs pa'i// bkra shis dam pa des 'dir bde leg shog/ 
297b5(1): skyob pa'i chos la legs pa'i tsho gas mnga' ba// shin du phan dang bde dang des gsungs pa// 'khor ba rtag bde mya ngan med thob pa'i// bkra shis dam pa des 'dir bde legs shog
297b6(1): dge 'dun che la mthu dpal rmanga' ba// bslab pa ni legs bcas brtson rnal 'byor can// bdag gzhan don tshon sbubs pa'i lam zhugs pa'i// bkra shis dam pa des 'dir bde legs shog
